<Author>hotelfanaticHK
<Content>The RP is alright! I heard about the Royal Plaza through TripAdvisor and picked it as my hotel of choice when booking my vacation through Zuji. Arriving at the hotel, just walking across the wonderfully-designed lobby made me feel like royalty. Check-in was very efficient and I was in my room with my bags in under 10 minutes. The property is ideally located on Scotts Roads, running perpendicular to Orchard Road, the shopping mecca of Singapore. There are many outlets and restaurants in the area, so you won't ever run out of places to shop or eat. Carousel, the restaurant in the lobby, arguably has one of the best halal buffets ever (the Sultan of Brunei owns this hotel and the Hyatt across the road). As for rooms, I was booked into a Superior. The room was minimally appointed, but the bathroom was nice and the bed was comfortable. There was a strange stench in the mini-bar, which was due to spilled milk and coffee that had not been cleaned before my arrival. The desk chair was also very uncomfortable due to an uneven seat. When I entered the room, the toilet seat was loose, so I had maintenance fix that immediately.All in all, it is a comfortable hotel, but I'm just a little picky about the quality of the rooms I stay in. Highly recommended =)  
<Date>Jan 3, 2009

<Author>catherinalove
<Content>Loved this hotel great hotel. not on orchard road, but a few steps away from it-- near enough to be almost part of orchard road, but distant enough to avoid excessive noise.we went on a december when orchard road was all lighted up and very pretty. near the hotel, there is a 24-hour mccafe if you get tired of local cuisine or need something familiar. orchard road is full of malls and shopping is good. the mrt is also very near, which is ideal and very convenient.the room was very nice. we got a club room. the bathroom was very modernly fitted and very nice--one of the nicest i've experienced so far. you can watch tv from the spacious tub while you're soaking. the toiletries are also complete and well packaged.sheets are very soft and bed comfortable. plus, the minibar, which is restocked daily with softdrinks, juices, water and beer, is free!the breakfast buffet is complete with both western and local food. choices were abundant. you can get samplings of singaporean food there. there is also a vegetarian menu.the bar and the musical entertainment is also nice. downside is that the entire hotel is non-smoking. but then, most of singapore have strict smoking policies.i love this hotel and would come back.

<Author>u07ch
<Content>had a good weeks stay This is a well loctated hotel if you are in town to shop as its close to the main shopping centres. If you are in town for work there are possibly better hotels for you - though the north-south mrt station is about 10 minutes walk away (in 34c heat.) Conveniently outside was a Starbucks if you want something better than the nescafe they provide in the room though the hotel has a rather nice looking coffee shop too.There were two issues that let my stay down; before i get to them the most important things with a singapore hotel (for me anyway): the bed was really comfortable, the shower was great and the air conditioning worked really well (though the controls are baffling all red and green lights.) Its a hotel well designed for business travelers with power sockets on the top of a large desk and internet access is included with the room rate. There were 3 easily accessibly power sockets in the room; one by the desk, one under the large tv and one under the bedside table. The first downside of my stay was that the internet access was terribly slow even something like uploading a couple of photos to flickr repeatedly failed; and the wireless disappeared completely for the last two days of my stay.The biggest upset was when i dropped something under the bed and had to look under it. There was room service food, pills and general mess which suggests that the cleanliness was more about appearance than substance. That surprised me because to that point I was impressed - the mains even folded my clothes into tidy piles when i left them on top of the desk chair.

<Author>grover71
<Content>Nice but overrated Stayed four nights. Problems at check in, they hadn't included our ten year old and wanted to charge an additional SD70 per night for a trundle bed. Lucky we had printed ALL email conversations. ***Make sure you take all email conversations!!!*** In the end they said they wouldn't charge us for the extra bed this time.Room was tidy and well decorated. Free minibar was not stocked with beer, had to ask for it. Was not used much anyway so was not real advantage, as it only consisted of 4 cans per day. Coke, Diet Coke, Tiger, Milo.The main advantage of this hotel is the enormous and very high quality breakfast. Usually SD32 a person if not included in the room price. However, food is very cheap and easily obtainable just a few steps in any direction out the door of the hotel. The problem with the breakfast is that we ate so much that we were not that hungry to eat all the other beautiful food available in Singapore - Hiannese Chicken Rice, Satay, etc etc etc.So overall, if the breakfast is the best thing about this hotel, you are better off saving your money and getting something a little cheaper, as this is a VERY expensive hotel for what it offers.

<Content>Enjoyable stay Booked 2 nights via their website for Premier (room only) and we were upgraded to the Royal Club floor - presumably bigger room, with buffet breakfast for 2 thrown in. Receptionist was very efficient, friendly and informative. Prompted us for our flight details for departure and recommended that we book a taxi for our early morning pick-up. Checkout was a breeze.Room decor is contemporary but I think the hallway to the rooms is getting a little tired. Have to bear in mind that this is a refurbished building. Bed was comfortable and blockout curtains a Godsend. Walls are a bit thin - I could hear people walking/talking in the hallway outside. Flatscreen tv, free wi-fi.Complimentary drinks in the mini bar is a nice touch but don't get too excited as it isn't stocked to the brim - 2 beers, 2 cans of softdrink, juice and water, restocked everyday. In-house restaurant, Carousel, is reknown for their sumptious high tea buffets on the weekends so do try. We did not get a chance to but it comes highly recommended from our local but the breakfast buffet had a nice spread.Great location. On the corner of Scotts and Orchard so you have the shopping and MRT station at your doorstep. Isetan shopping centre is next door with a grocery store if you need anything else. Heaps of fastfood restaurants nearby - some even 24 hours.Concierge was helpful in booking an early morning taxi for our departure.Rate a little expensive but it is hard to find a cheaper hotel without compromising location and rating.Would stay again if the rates don't creep up.

<Author>dalton1skiing
<Content>Great location, small rooms We stayed 1 week as it was the only accomodation we could find. Our holiday coincided with the first ever Formula 1 in Singapore when hotel prices went through the roof. Although we had a terrific holiday, this hotel was not my 1st choise, actually my 5th, but the others were booked out for the F1. The outside is unimpressive and looks nothing like a hotel. Right next to a DFS deparment store which looked grander. The entrance area looks impressive, but has no baring on the rooms appearance or rest of the hotel. Reception was efficient  had our booking, all went smoothly. The entire hotel is smoke free. It must also be owned by Muslims as the menus had only 'turkey ham' and 'beef bacon'. There is also a Qaran in the bedside desk. Other than these, there were no other obvious indicators that is was owned/run by muslims.  The room was smaller than expected. We got the standard (i think they call it the deluxe!) which doesnt include the free mini-bar and breakfast. That was an option when booking, but the added amount to have breakfast included was ridiculous. When we checked in, we were given the option again of adding breakfast each day at $28 singapore dollars +++. The +++ adds an extra 17% to the total bill for tax and service charge. You cant just have it 1 or 2 days of the breakfast, you must have it the entire stay. If you only want a few days breakfast there, its $32 +++. I do love the all you can eat style breakfast, but I certainly dont eat $37 worth. Esp when nearby local food halls have terrific food for $3! I had forgoten how expensive Singapore is when compared to say Thailand or Malaysia. Our room had 2 large (almost double sized) twin beds with very comfy, thick mattresses and extra long pillows. A large, flat screen TV and small fridge. Hairdryer, safe, iron and ironing board and plenty of mirrors including a full length one. The bathroom was very small too with just a shower. There was a normal sized shower head, and an absolutely enormous one too. Hot water was no problem. We occasionally could hear a door closing nearby, but never heard noise, tv or voices from either neighbouring rooms. The reading lights actually face down from the roof so blind your eyes. Very uncomfortable to read with. The TV has several English channels including 2 movie channels, several sports, BBC, CNN, Discovery, a few in Mandarin, 1 french, 1 Italian, 1 German, 1 from Brunei and a few from Malaysia.  There was an adaptor for free internet, although we didnt bring out lap tops. Also a multi-plug adaptor fitted into the wall which was handy. I dont think any of the rooms have a particularity good view. We could see Scotts road by peering out. The windows didnt open and there is no balcony. There is a kettle with tea/coffee facilities of sorts. 2 tea bags, 2 sachets of coffee, 2 sugar sachets and only 1 mini-milk sachet in the fridge. The milk was only topped up on the 4th day and the others bits randomly. I had bought a small carton of milk at a 7 eleven by that stage. They also supplied 2x 600ml water bottles, but again these were random and not supplied every day like I suspect they are supposed to be. They weren't there initially and only turned up on day 2. The room was kept very clean whilst there. Sheets and towels changed when requested. Staff were always curtious, helpful and smiled. There is a buisiness lounge on the 2nd floor. Reception advised us (on day 5 of our stay!) that we were entiltled to 15mins free internet useage each. I ended up using it several times and was told that as long as no one was waiting, I could stay on using it and not restricted to just 15mins. The location of the hotel is very good. 2mins to orchard road  the MRT. Lots of local restaurants and shops to choose from. Room service and restaurant prices were terrible though. The pool was small for a so called 5 star hotel and the surrounding decked area became very full during the day. We requested late check out as our flight wasnt till 9pm. This wasnt granted, even though we offered to pay extra. (Due to the F1 booking out the hotel). We were able to shower in the pool showers, but this had no chair in the shower area,  not any room to relax and wait. We were told that they were considering adding some sort of comfort area for this in the future, as other customers had complained. When or if such a room will be provided, who knows. I woud stay there again if the room prices were good, but there are more reasonably priced hotels which include breakfast and have better facilities in the vicinity.  
<Date>Sep 30, 2008

<Author>teqp
<Content>Very nice place to stay and close to Orchard Road. This is our first stop for our Singapore/Indonesia trip. After a LONG 18 hour flight from Los Angeles (transit at Taipei), we arrived at Singapore. We only stayed there for one night before heading to our Indonesia diving/snorkeling trip. We were both tired and just wanted to check-in the hotel and rest. We told the receptionist that we want a quiet room and were given an upgrade to their deluxe room with see-through window connecting the bathroom and bedroom. The room is nice with all the 4 star hotel amenities (plasma TV, 320-thread-count Egyptian cotton comforter), but the real standout is the free mini-bar and nice bathtub with separate shower. My girlfriend enjoyed her bubble bath especially after a long flight. The bath tub is decent size, and you can watch TV from the tub (through see-through glass), but can鈥檛 hear it too well or change the channel because the TV is not in the bathroom. If you want some privacy in the bathroom, no problem, there is a blind you can pull down in the bathroom to cover the glass. The separate shower is decent size too, you have plenty of room in the shower (compared to Hilton, which is a separate report), and the best is the huge overhead shower head. It鈥檚 the size of basketball which has really good water pressure too (very relaxing after a long flight). The free mini bar consists of roughly 10 bottles of drinks (2 tiger bears, 2 water, 2 juices, coke, diet coke, Milo), sorry memory is fading, should鈥檝e taken a picture of it. It is a very nice touch and most hotels would probably charge you $30 for all those drinks. Oh, forgot to mention, you can use their computer at business center for free the first 15 minutes. The only thing I don鈥檛 like about Royal Plaza is they charge you $5.20 Singapore dollars for advance booking a taxi for you. Our flight next morning was at 9:25am, so we need a taxi 7am in the morning and was afraid that we couldn鈥檛 get a taxi that early in the morning if we don鈥檛 book in advance. But I think you can just call the concierge early in the morning and have them call a taxi for you, and that鈥檚 free of charge. For the price we paid for on expedia.com: $150 including tax, we would definitely stay there again.

<Author>dan55
<Content>Average, not great Lovely foyer  location hides an average hotel.On the whole, this place wasn't really that bad. However, a combination of a lot of little things put us off going back. Have a read of my pluses/minuses and see what you think.Good things about the hotel1. Location is awesome: Close to MRT (subway), major shops, food, taxi2. The free broadband was excellent. Fast, low latency. I was using the supplied Ethernet cable which I would recommend over wireless.3. The taxi guy out the front was good.4. 'What can I do for you' service was OK, fairly prompt when requesting ice.5. The king size bed was super comfy (pillows were not heaven for me or my wife).6. Was upgraded to the Deluxe Corner room which is slightly larger than Deluxe (thank you for that).Bad things about the hotel1. Fair is fair, the free minibar is actually free, no catches when it comes to paying.However, there is still a catch!A normal minibar depending where you stay would contain:2 to 8 snacks4 to 10 mini spirit bottles2 to 4 juices2 to 6 beers (usually 2-3 different types)This absolutely free minibar contains: 0 Snacks0 mini spirit bottles2 juices2 small cans of Tiger beerAltogether that is about 8 SGD worth of drinks. It is NOT false advertising, but definitely deceptive.2. To top off the free mini-bar being a dud, it wasn't even stocked consistently. I drank my juice the first two days and was then hooked on having a nice morning juice, the next 7 days after that it was never restocked. Poor.3. The lighting in the room we stayed in (Deluxe Corner) was poor, they need reading lights so you can set the mood for reading/tv/etc. You turn on the overhead bed lights are you blinded by giant Halogen floodlights.4. Let's face it, even though you don't go on holiday to watch TV, sometimes you end up watching it while you wait for a place to open or while relaxing in the room.Free to air offerings were fine. Pay movies were non-existent even though we wanted to watch something.5. Hotel has those giant 'king sized' pillows. I asked for foam instead, they took two goes for them to bring something that was actually foam. Still huge, however sufficient to let me and my wife to get some sleep. Could have been a better experience.6. Shower, we didn't enjoy, needle spray, needs a shower curtain or door, water went all over the floor.7. An ice machine would be nice so I don't have to call up when I run out, proper drinking glasses rather than toothbrush holder glasses also.8. The maid forgot to give us a spare toilet roll on more than one occasion (we did run out and had to phone them).9. Room service isn't just expensive like most hotels, it is insanely expensive. Especially for Singapore where you can get a nice meal from a hawker centre for $3.

<Author>tei1988
<Content>Would go back. Stayed at the RP for 6 nights: was back in Singapore to attend a reunion and visit family. Location was my primary reason: it's close to all the activity of Orchard Road, but also just outside the restricted zone of Orchard Road (i.e. the restricted zone taxes vehicles at certain times which will affect taxi prices).Staff were friendly and helpful. I stayed on the 8th floor; no view, but I didn't need it. Room was of a decent size. My king size bed was actually two twins put together, and I could feel the dent between the two. But since I was there alone, this wasn't an issue.Pool and gym are open at a 6.00am: all of us suffering from jetlag were there. Pool is small but refreshing. Gym's treadmills had tv screens on them, which was a novelty for me!RP is within walking distance to the trains (MRT) and buses. Starbucks is just outside, to your right. Shopping is everywhere! If you want to give local food a go, head towards Wisma Atria (big blue building, to your right on Orchard Road). There's a food court on the 4th floor at reasonable prices called The Food Republic.RP is also known for its High Tea on weekends, and the locals will line up for it.The room was clean but it wasn't pristine. I had no complaints though, and overall: would go back for the price offered. A good value.

<Author>Sophie_Spain
<Content>Good value for money - but not a dream experience Stayed 3 nights at the Royal Plaza on Scotts in July, as part of our honeymoon.Location is fantastic, cannot be better located in Singapore.Service is OK, pero nothing special against Asian standards. Booked a Club/ executive room, was given a room on floor 13, not big at all for a superior room, no fancy decoration, not very luxurious in general. Bathroom was new and very clean (also pretty small). The views from the rooms are not good, be prepared. Minibar is free.Executive room have access to the lounge on floor 15, good food and beverages and nice atmosphere.Breakfast in the ground floor is a disaster, too many people, hot food is served cold, not a nice experience in general, would not recommend it.Tough policy with late check-outs. However let us do a late check-out because hotel was not full, which was a very appreciated detail. Also had a couple of other details for our honeymoon.With regard to transportation, do not use the hotel airport limousine, it costs 85 SGD whereas a normal limousine costs about 30 and is perfectly fine.

<Author>SueinNZ
<Content>Not so positive about the plaza I chose this hotel for my Singapore stay as the location seemed good (near Orchard Road) and there was a possibility of a reasonably-priced club room, with a lounge offering free internet access. I'm not sure if I made the right decision on either count. Firstly, I think I was wrong about the location- Singapore tourist life seems to be moving nearer to the harbour nowadays and so, if you wanted to do anything, you had to take the MRT or a taxi. Secondly, I have mixed feelings about the club room. On the plus side- the view was fine, despite what previous reviewers have said; the room was a decent size and there were very good in-room amenities; the club lounge offered a good breakfast and even afternoon tea, which was impressive on the one occasion I could try it. On the negative side- I had chosen a club room specifically so that I would be able to check in to my flight at 10.55pm, the 24 hours advance notice that BA seems to need if you are going to get a decent seat. When I turned up at the lounge at 10.45pm, I was immediately told somewhat curtly by no fewer than two members of staff that they were about to close-even though no mention of a closing time had been made earlier. I enquired further and found that the lounge in fact shut at 11pm. When I said that I would be finished and out by then, this did not seem to go down well. I was as good as my word and left by 11pm but the episode left a bad taste. I said as much in my customer survey. When the Duty manager wanted to see me after I had checked out, I thought that it might be to express some regret for the previous night. Not at all- it was to ask me if I had taken a bath robe, as house keeping had reported one missing fron my room! (I had assumed that I was meant to have only been given one robe, as I was staying on my own). As you can imagine, the various benefits which I've mentioned above don't quite make up for the feeling that I was given of being a) an inconvenience and b) a thief!

<Author>murray_maccoll
<Content>Can't fault it We were returning to Australia from the UK and decided to stop over in Singapore for three days to do some exploration. With a three year old and a six month old my wife and I were desperate to ensure that the hotel we stayed at was set up for the unique requirements of a family eg fridge for baby food, friendly and understanding staff, cots etc. At the Royal Plaza on Scotts we found everything we needed and more.The staff were outstanding and very friendly. What's more we never once felt like having children was an inconvenience to either the other guests or the staff.The location is ideal for access to Orchard road and the bus that goes directly to the Singapore Zoo (highly recommended) stops right outside twice a day. If we ever find ourselves back in Singapore for even the shortest stay we will definitely be returning to the Royal Plaza on Scotts.

<Author>water_lili_88
<Content>Fantastic hotel in great location I stayed in this hotel for two days. Booked a deluxe room and was upgraded to Premier room. Although the view is not great (facing car park), this is true of Singapore city hotels generally. The hotel service was fantastic. <Author>sss1970t
<Content>Super Location, Ambience...stay there often From the time you enter the hotel, it smells and feels fresh and clean. Its a non-smoking hotel, but has about a 150 tea-lights in the lobby! ironic!The check in is very fast, and with a smile.The rooms have everything you need. Clean, good size by Singapore standards, but the view is that of a car-park. Personally, i preferred the rooms before the make over of the hotel.Where this hotel really scores is the free inroom internet, free minibar, and the absolutely fantastic location. You can walk most places, to the MRT as well. Further, there is a covered escalator bridge between the hotel and Far East Plaza across the road. Hence, you have the flexibility to hire a taxi from either direction. Given the Singapore rain and traffic, this itself saves 10 minutes per trip, and is great if you're on work like i was and had many meetings.The check out process was a bit erratic. Please confirm the rate you book at as well as other booking details, as there could be confusion at check out. My friends too experienced the same problem.Staff is polite and efficient, room service and breakfast is good. Didn't try any restaurant, as there are many better cheaper ones in singapore.

<Content>Perfect location. Stayed here between May 30th till June 2nd. We booked the deluxe room with an extra bed. However upon check-in, we were upgraded to the slightly spacious corner deluxe at no extra cost. Loved the location. RIght next to the shops, restaurants etc. I have previously stayed at this hotel before the renovations so was looking forward to staying there again. Loved the fact that it is a smoke-free hotel as my son has asthma.I also chose the hotel because the food served was Halal, a big plus for me. Even when we were sick of hotel food, we could just go across to Far East Plaza for some good halal Malay Thai food.Hotel staff were friendly and extremely helpful especially the Concierge Mr. Ibrahim.There are shuttle services to go to the Singapore Zoo and Night Safari right outside the hotel.The room was spacious enough to fit an extra bed for my son. We missed the last breakfast(much to my son's disappointment).Having said that, I will definately stay here again. Am already making plans for Christmas!

<Author>julie072
<Content>Well worth staying at this great hotel Have just returned from a 4 night stay at this hotel.If I were to return to Singapore - this would be my pick again. This was the 10th trip to Singapore and this hotel was probably the best I have stayed, especially the location. Scotts Road is a buzz of activity and so convenient. I had good intentions to travel via the MRT, but in the end travelled everywhere via taxi. Too convenient when there is one waiting right at the front door for you everytime you step out.The staff were very unintrusive, and I did not have a lot to do with them apart from the 2 minute check in and out. The room was small but roomy enough especially since we didnt spend that much time there. We had twin beds which are equivalent to a small double bed. I left a list for housekeeping ( a long list mind you) and they accommodated and gave us everything on the list.Now the little gripes - The kettle in our room was terrible and had to be boiled twice and there was no clock which was a bit of a pain. Take your own hairdryer as the one supplied is attached inside the bedside drawer and the on button had to be held down constantly.... this was very annoying.The curtains are great though - block out which keeps the room nice and dark. I cant rave about the buffet breakfast.... very very ordinary compared to other hotel buffets I have had, but ample enough. I would not pay extra for the breakfast (we had it included in our rate) as there is food very close by. I loved the fact that MCDonalds - MCCafe was right next door as I could get my coffee fix regularly. The buffet finishes at 10am which I think is too early - especially when you are in no rush to get up in the morning as the shops dont open till 10-11am.The free water and drinks was a great bonus as there is not really a supermarket that close to buy these things. There is a shopping centre across the road - Far East Plaza which was very convenient and had great shopping-- better than the expense of Orchard Road.So, I would definately return and recommend this hotel.

<Author>ozmadmax
<Content>Nice cold shower in the morning! The hotel is in a good location for shopping and entertainment around Orchard Road so good for tourists. I stayed here on a one night stopover whilst on business.Check-in was ok, I was repeatedly advised that the hotel is strictly non-smoking (which I wouldn't have known becuase I couldn't have seen the half dozen signs in reception telling me and the declaration of a $300 per day fee for cleaning the room in the event that I did smoke on the check-in form). Despite this I was asked to sign an acceptance of this condition despite it not being mentioned at the time of booking. Regardless I was happy to sign as I do not smoke and hate being in a non-smoking room where somebody has smoked so this was all very acceptable if not unorthodox.The room was pleasant enough, modern furnishing, a bit of a dank smell (combination of aircon and lack of ventilation of fresh air). Window faced onto another building so no sunlight. Internet connection was free so this was a real plus as I was on business. The free minibar is ok (not quite a minibar, more of a mini-minibar but hey it was free so I'll leave it there).The bathroom is quite small and poorly laid out (don't expect to use the bidet as there is no water pressure). The whole bathroom thing got worse the following morning. I rose early to catch my onward flight (6am) to discover that there was no hot water. I thought at first that it would just get warmer and I hopped in. Alas it was freezing for the entire shower so I woke up very quickly. When checking out I mentioned this and was told that I was in a corner room so it takes a while to heat up. There was no apology, no response to how long does it take to heat up unlike the repeated references to smoking at check-in. I therefore decided to give this hotel a miss for future trips as I like a hot (even a warm) shower in the mornings. Whilst the hotel was quite modern, it appears to lack soul. The service is a bit perfunctory and there was little or no personal touch even when problems occur. Better than some and if you like a cold shower then highly recommended.

<Content>An enjoyable experience! This is a very good hotel and I would certainly stay here again (I could rate it as excellent, but I'm becoming more conservative in my ratings). It is situated right in the heart of a lot of good shopping and dining establishments and is very convenient to public transit - some of the most efficient in the world. The room itself was spacious and very comfortable and included a free minibar. Regrettably, the fitness center was being renovated while I was there (the fitness center was one of the reasons I booked there), but that was a minor inconvenience. The staff is very attentive, pleasant and courteous. While I didn't get to visit their Carousel restaurant, it looked very nice and I will probably dine there during my next visit. The hotel lobby is quite spacious and beautiful. While I was there, they had a large display of tea candles that many guest were getting photos taken in front of. They also had a display of art by local artists - all of which were quite good. Good enough to be too expensive for me, though. I would recommend the Royal Plaza to friends and plan to stay there for my next visit.

<Author>johnsmith47
<Content>Great hotel on Orchard Road in Singapore I booked my stay directly with the hotel. I got a much better rate than the big travel sites, and it included an enormous breakfast buffet. The room was well furnished with a roomy and well equipped bath. It had a separate shower stall, but it had a waterfall showerhead and a hand held head. The hotel was quiet. The staff was great, especially Ibrahim at the concierge desk. The location was perfect. The MTR subway stop was a block away. There is an amazing amount of shopping and dining on Orchard Road. Taxis are very cheap, about S$16 from the airport to the hotel. The taxi drivers put the pedal to the metal, so hold on. The MTR line will take you to the downtown area. The hotel bar has a live band most of the nights. The lobby was was nicely decorate. There is free internet access at the business center for 15 minutes, if you need a pc to check email. There is also somone to help you with faxes and other things.

<Author>JP724
<Content>Great stay at Royal Plaza on Scotts, even with teenagers! A family holiday for us (family of 5) normally means staying in budget-priced motels/resorts. The kids are getting older and probably won't be holidaying with us much longer, so this year we splashed out with a 10-day stay in Singapore and chose the Royal Plaza on Scotts. Despite booking 7 months in advance, this was the only hotel that I could find that had two rooms available on the same dates for such a long stay. I ended up booking directly through their website, which was easy and straightforward. A few weeks before our stay they emailed me, asking if we had any special requirements. I reminded them that we required adjoining rooms and an extra bed in one of the rooms and they confirmed that this had been noted.Upon arrival, check-in was quick and easy. We were put on the 5th floor, handy for the swimming pool. Rooms were adjoining and a reasonable size with king-size beds. Previous experience (on other holidays) led us to expect the kids to argue over who was going to sleep in the crappy, tiny rollaway bed - but no, here in this hotel the bed has a proper mattress and was a standard size single bed, so all children were able to sleep comfortably. The bed was made up ready for our late arrival but we had to remind them to bring an extra set of towels, this was done within minutes of our request. The suitcases were brought up quickly too. The rooms only had showers, not a problem with our older children, but might be if you had little ones to bath each night.The rooms were very clean, bathrooms were always clean, all-in-all we couldn't fault the housekeeping service. The kids loved the way their pj's were folded up neatly for them and teddies placed on pillows! The mini-bars were topped up daily (complimentary beer and soft drinks). On the first day I left a note asking that no beer be put in the kids fridge, instead they replenished the fridge with extra soft drinks. We always had plenty of soft drinks/water bottles to take out with us on our sightseeing trips, so this was very handy. The staff noticed that we were big tea drinkers and always left extra tea bags and milks. We only needed to ring down to reception with one small problem during our stay; the remote control wasn't working and needed new batteries and this was fixed straightaway. There was no view from the window but we were never in the room long enough to worry about that.To use the lifts and to get back to your room from the swimming pool, you have to remember to carry your keycard with you at all times, but they do give you 2 for each room. The swimming pool was about 15metres long, so ok for lap-swimming, ideal for kids cooling off, plenty of sunloungers and towels available. Clean changing rooms and toilets, and a sauna available. A function room is located on the other side of the pool and this was often in use, but for the staff and business people to get to it, they had to walk along the edge of the pool, which seems to me poor planning and could be dangerous due to the permanently wet floor, especially with the waiters walking back and forth with food and crockery. It was a little off-putting sun-bathing in a bikini with gents in business suits walking back and forth during breaks.The hotel rooms were pricey, but no more than other similar hotels in Singapore, and it's a fact of life for those families with 3 children that you always have to fork out for 2 rooms. So to pay $30+ per person for breakfast each morning, wasn't going to happen! We're not fast-food people, but on this occasion it was very handy that there is a McDonald's and a McCafe located just a few metres up the street. Just a bit further up is the entrance to the MRT, very handy. Outside the hotel, getting a taxi was never a problem, with porters always ready to wave one in for you. Going back into the lobby after a day's sightseeing was always welcoming, it looks so bright and clean with very cool air-conditioning and it always looked lovely at night with the candles lit up.Upon check-out there were no discrepancies with the bill, no extra charges to query which is always a relief. I wouldn't hesitate to recommend this hotel to family and friends and would gladly stay there again.  
<Date>Apr 29, 2008

<Author>RosieFlynn
<Content>great stay at Royal Plaza again.. I'm just back from my second stay at the Royal Plaza.Both times were for business, so I'm not sure how the holiday traveller will find the hotel...I found whole experience pleasent and the staff very friendly and helpful. The rooms were a good size and the complimentary internet and mini bar a nice touch for Singapore.The bathrooms are nice with sufficiant toiletries for long haul destination, should your luggage get delayed there's enough here to keep you going.The location is also a great plus point if you are looking for a hotel in the middle of the hustle and bustle and, of course shopping, of Orchard.There's plenty of eating options around, and one of my favourite vegatarian restaurants is just a short walk away!..Singapore is such a safe place I've never felt uncomfortable as a lone female traveller walking around alone after dark. However if you happen to be near the Hyatt or Mariott across the road you'll notice the presence of prostitutes hanging around outside the hotels, which may make you feel uncomfortable...coming from Amsterdam, I'm not bothered....but I've witnessed none of this at the Royal Plaza.The gym facilites are pretty small here, one tredmill, bike, step machine, weight maching and free weights. Which is fine and I've only ever been the 2nd or 3rd person in the there, but I do miss the sauna/steam facilities that are usually found in 4/5 star hotels in Singapore, especiall after the long flight.Overall I would (and have) recommend this hotel, the price is good, but I have noticed it rise since my last visit. I fthis continues I think I'll go back to the Hyatt as the facilities are much more varied...which is what you pay for.

<Author>Garthy_2
<Content>Great location and lounge This is a great value four-star hotel. We opted for the Club floor which was great value. The rooms were modern and functional with free wireless internet. Air con was good but slightly noisy. Free brekky in the lounge and also free evening cocktails with great food-you can even skip dinner esp if you also attend the afternoon tea! There were desserts and fresh fruits and hot canapes with free drinks-great value. Free beer and soft drinks in mini bar was great for a day of exploring and shopping. The rate was one of the cheapest in the Orchard Rd area - beautiful X'mas lights. None of the rooms have great views but ours with the pool view was among the best I suspect as the building faces up Scotts Rd rather than fronts it. Breakfast downstairs was really busy but not bad variety of local and usual food. Fresh fruits were great. There was a noodle bar as well. Hotel is smoke free completely and pork free as well! Taxis were at the door and Singapore has world's best practice and greatest value. Cost about S$17 to get the four of us to the Zoo! Easy to cross overhead pedestrian bridge to FarEast Shopping Centre and on to Orchard Rd rather than battle the underground passage or breathe the air at the lights- just turn left at the front door. Recommend Straits Kitchen at the Grand Hyatt for upmarket local and pan-Asianfood, all you can eat for less than S$50 done in superb fashion and surroundings. Tang's Dept Store has great value esp. of sales items.

<Author>FussyGlobeTrotter
<Content>Club room represents great value for drinkers! I am writing this review from inside my room - using the free internet provided and getting ready for the cocktail hour starting shortly. Because I'm already here and don't need to worry about getting a booking I feel I can let you in on a great deal in Singapore.(Can be tough to make a reservation here, as since the recent renovations and their 'Carousel' restaurant winning the best newcomer buffet for 2007 award, this hotel is quickly growing in popularity) I travel with my husband a lot for work, and between us we have visited many other hotels in Singapore before finding this one including: The Meritus Mandarin (incredibly noisy and appalling service) Copthorne Kings (simply awful) Novotel Clarke Quay (OK, but just another hotel nothing special) Marina Mandarin (was OK, but have not gone back) Hilton (needs serious refurbishment and quickly) and many others that I can't even remember now....So, on with the story.The Royal Plaza on Scotts keeps drawing us back as it represents good value for money (talking about club room deal), is in the centre of town right near Orchard Road for shopping and keeps us both happy.It has recently been refurbished, so all of the rooms feel clean and new with flat screen TV's, king sized beds, a comfy blue velour chair in the corner to throw your clothes over. lol. and the bathrooms feel clean and have a separate bath and shower (a must in my books. I do not take showers in a bath). There is a glass wall between the bedroom and bathroom so the room feels bigger (can pull down a blind don't worry) and everything just works.You get free internet throughout the entire hotel at all hours (wi-fi or cable, with cables provided in the room if you're not up with the latest technology). This level of service is great and means I can relax by the pool with my laptop if I want to.The pool is pretty basic as is the gym, but that's not why we stay here. We come here for the club room food and drinks deal.We always upgrade to the club room for an extra $60 per day for two of us which gets us the following: 6.30am - 10am - Full breakfast either served in the club room upstairs (if you want to avoid the rif-raff) or downstairs in the public breakfast lobby if you want slightly more choices, as the buffet is huge. There is a full cooked section with eggs any way you like, pancakes, waffles, curries, fish, mash potato, noodles, chinese dumplings, congee... you get the picture. A cold section with fruits, cereal, yoghurt and a bakery section with pastries. Coffee and tea is free flowing as are the many juices. 3pm-5pm - Afternoon tea served upstairs in the club room (no rif-raff). More hot food selections like noodles, prawns, fried dumplings as well as cakes, scones, cream, jams, lemon butter, desserts, fruit, water, tea and coffee. BTW, when I say water we're talking bubbly Perrier served in a glass with ice and a slice of lime, not tap.This is the best bit...5.30pm-8pm - Cocktail time!!! Served in the club room, with all of the other happy guests. Fab hot and cold canapes served on spoons and mini dishes just like at a nice function - all alongside a table of breads, cheeses and desserts. The menu changes every night and for example last night some of the cold spoons were smoked salmon rolls topped with sour cream and chives,thai influenced beef rolls, chicken breast with tomato salsa dressing and the hot dishes were sauteed fish with lemon butter sauce and capers, mini lasagnes and prawn skewers wrapped in turkey bacon with a triad of sauces. AND ALL OF THIS IS SERVED WITH FREE FLOW SPARKLING WINE, WHITE WINE, RED WINE, BEER and BASIC SPIRITS for the 2.5 hour duration. Ths is very exciting to drinkers like us who pay a minimum of AUS$60 for a bottle of wine out at dinner in Singapore. Between the two of us we easily make our club room money back on drinks during cocktail hour and we can't recommend this deal enough for drinkers visiting Singapore. (If you haven't been to Singapore before and you're a foodie from Melbourne, prepare to die at the price of wine and 'high end' food BTW)In fact, we often make reservations for dinner and come 8pm, we cancel because we are completely stuffed from the canapes....So there you have it. The club room deal just keeps us coming back again and again! Hope this review has helped!

<Author>Bandi07
<Content>Great location, and very reasonably priced. I often stay at the Royal Plaza in Singapore, and it has grown better over time. Recently the rooms have been refurbished and now have flat-screen TVs and new furnishings. Internet is free, and minibar is free too (2 beers and a few soft drinks). That's like slicing $30 off the price. The breakfast buffet is excellent, staff are very friendly and helpful, and security is good (you need to use your room key to access the guest floors in the elevator). The location is also great, as it is just 100m from the corner of Orchard and Scotts Roads. Lots of shopping centers all around. The view from the room is not so great if you are on a low floor, as you only see the building next door. Higher floors may be better, I've never paid the higher rate to find out.I much prefer the Royal Plaza over the Orchard or Orchard Parade hotels, which are in the same area and similar in price. The Hilton and the Negara hotels are also in the same area, and are better but considerably more expensive. I've stayed in all of them, and Royal Plaza is my top pick.

<Author>meyeti
<Content>Royal Plaza on Scotts - Highly Recommended for Business Travelers Recently stayed at the Royal Plaza on Scotts for business meetings in Singapore. As a business hotel, it's one of the best I've been in. Room quality was excellent, free wireless internet, free mini-bar (2 local beers, soft drinks, water) and a nice breakfast buffet. Since it was booked by my local host company, the rate was very good (S$220/night plus taxes). Staff was very polite and went out of their way to accommodate my requests. As I had a midnight flight back to Europe, I asked for late checkout. I was allowed to check out at 8PM for S$100- supplementary charge. After 14:00, normally S$20/hour and a full day charged after 6PM. So I appreciated greatly the possibility to have a full day of activity, come back and shower before heading to the airport. Only two minor minus points - the view from my window was of a wall facing the hotel and there was only a shower in the bathroom. Not a problem for me, but if you're looking for a soak after a long day, best to ask for a room with a tub. I had whatever they call their standard room.

<Author>BizTraveller07
<Content>Great for Business Travellers I have stayed at this Hotel on previous visits to Singapore.This time I arrived fairly late in the evening (11pm) and after the lady on check in tried to put me into a room with single beds it was agreed that it really wasn't my problem if they had given someone else my room and that they would upgrade me to a Superior room. The check in process was actually quite painless and handled well.The room was great (especially as it was an upgrade), well appointed, very clean and very comfortable.The Hotel is in great shape and combined with it's location it makes for a great place for a business travel. They have always been happy to do it if they aren't fully booked and they only charge around S$20 per extra hour for check outs past 2 or 3 pm - well worth it if you have a long flight ahead.

<Author>Human44
<Content>Great room; lousy entrance Stayed here for a week's business trip. The room was clean, quiet and with excellent bedding. If your primary goal is to get a good night's sleep at a reasonable cost, then this is the place to stay in Singapore.With coffee  tea making facility, plus the juice in the free mini-bar, room service breakfast is quite a reasonable alternative to the buffet restaurant below. I never ate there during my stay, but used room service for waffles and croissants/toast/muffins at a fraction of the cost.The hotel's biggest downside is the dreadful entrance - not the nice enough lobby, but the under-construction driveway and curb area outside the front door. They have fenced off the pedestrian walkway that connects easily to the adjacent DFS shopping arcade, meaning that the only way to walk in/out of the hotel is through a driveway that's often jammed with cars, buses and trucks. For all the traffic at the front door, it's not always easy to get a taxi. On my return to Changi airport, the only vehicle that pulled up in 10 minutes of waiting was an Airport Taxi which charged roughly double the regular cab fare. Don't get into anything other than a metered taxi unless you're ready to pay double for your airport trip.

<Author>coxfamily3
<Content>Loved it, good value! We stayed at the Royal Plaza for 8 nights and stayed in the Executive Suite as we travelled with a 3yo and 7month old. Our room was on the 10th floor, these suite go from the 10th to 15th floors. Our room entailed a separate lounge (which is where we put the cot and rollaway bed for the children) which had a large screen TV, a lounge suite and 2 tub chairs, writing desk and coffee table and also a dining table.Our bedroom was very roomy with an iron and ironing board and his/hers wardrobes. It had a king bed with large marble ensuite with bath and separate shower and also a bidet.The turn down service is great in the evenings as they replenish all used towels and fill your ice bucket, empty bins and even tidy your bed etc The views were of surrounding buildings but was a very quiet room with good natural light.We had tea/coffee making facilities and free mini bar which has 2 Tiger beers, 3 cans of Soft Drink, an orange juice and 4 bottles of water daily, which was great.We also got a complimentary choice of buffet meal daily at Carousel and entry to the Royal Club lounge. We chose breakfast and dinners on alternating days, then mid week decided on dinners instead and they happily complied! The range of buffet food was fantastic from sushi, to seafood including prawns and crayfish to Wagyu beef , Duck and Quail- also various roasted meats and a large asian choice. The desserts were fantastic- there really was something for everyone and breakfast just as amazing in choice.We didnt use the Royal Club until a few days before we left as we had the kids, but that was a mistake as we had free breakfast , afternoon tea, all day tea/coffee/soft drinks and evening cocktails which run from 5.30 to 8pm (my husband really enjoyed the cognac!) it was a great place to go together or separately for a bit of quiet!. It is on the 15th floor and the lifts are very fast, so not a problem to get to.We didnt try the wifi but used the complimentary computers.The Pool was a typical hotel pool, but the gym was small but is going to be upgraded this year. Was absolutely a first class, 5 star hotel, but saying that ,we had a mix of business people and families and didnt feel out of place with 2 young children.The staff were friendly and courteous, check in was fast, the door men were knowledgable in everything we asked them, from laundromats to directions!Hotel is very well placed for MRT access and in the heart of Orchard Rd. Also has a supermarket within 100metres.We hired a babysitter for our children for 2hrs in the evening and they are from the hotel- from housekeeping etc so this was organised through the hotel and was $9 per hour (3hr min) for however many children. We will definately stay here again and would recommend the Club Lounge.

<Author>FeedTheFishMayo
<Content>Interesting I booked this hotel for the first 3 nights of a 5 night stay, as the last 2 nights were paid for at the Pan Pacific. I selected this hotel based on the review sbut when I arrived I was initially disappointed. The lobby looked great in the photos but was a bit dated when inspected in person. Staff were very helpful but when I got to the room I thought it was a bit small. The room had been recently renovated and all the fittings were good. The bathroom was spacious but the room had a very strange feature. There was a huge window from the bathroom into the main room. There is a blind that you can pull down for privacy but the issue is a night, if one person goes to the bathroom and turns on the light then the entire room is filled with light. If you want a room with a view, good luck. I would check when you book your room as the only room with a view are the front rooms that face Scott St. Internet access was free, which was great and the hotel is well located for people planning to shop around Orchard Road as it can be hard to grab a cab in the area on the weekend but you can walk back to your hotel. Also the free mini bar was a nice feature. If you want to base yourself near restaurants then I would pick somewhere else. This place is a good location for shopping and bars/nighclubbing.An interesting point is that this hotel is owned by the Sultan of Brunei, so it tends to have a large percentage of Muslim guests. You will find a copy of the Qur'an instead of a bible. This is not a criticism - just an observation.I moved from this hotel to the Pan Pacific where the rooms were much bigger, with great views, but were far more dated and they charged for internet access, etc. If I was going back I would probably choose Royal Plaza for value over the Pan Pacific.

<Author>shining_light
<Content>Decent and good value I thought the hotel was well worth the price. It is in such an excellent location - close to shops, food and transport. I cannot fault the service. Staff were always polite and helpful. The doormen were fantastic - always ready to open a door or hail a taxi or greet you as you return from a full day of sight-seeing. I have to say the lobby was impressive and it was nice to wander through the paintings on display. We had a small problem on arrival as we had requested a room with twin beds but were given a room with two beds made up as a king bed. The housekeeping staff were efficient in re-making the beds as we had requested. Our room was on the 7th floor facing a multistorey carpark and the back of another building however since we didn't spend much time in our room, the lack of view wasn't an issue. The free minibar was appreciated at the end of a hot day and having free access to internet service (even for just 15 minutes) was great. We found the room clean and enjoyed the comforts of modern furnishings and bathroom. I would probably have put the hairdryer in a more convenient location - not tucked into a tight spot in the room. It was great to be able to step out of the hotel and be within metres of shops. It's good to learn the underground routes around the Scotts and Orchard Rds area as it keeps you out of the heat and the tropical rain. These tunnels keep you connected to many of the major shopping centres and food courts in the area. If i go back to Singapore I would definitely go back to Royal Plaza and I recommend it to anyone.

<Author>Philosann
<Content>great location for shopaholics My wife and I have stayed at the Royal Plaza 3 times this year and there's no doubt that overall it's very good value for money, having been refurbished in early 07 means that the rooms are efficient, clean and modern if a little on the small side in the bathroom - watch out those of you who like a bath as the de-luxe only had a shower but the premi猫re had both and separately, the shower is of good size and has a choice of small shower head or enormous. Good choice of toileteries and proper bath sized towels.The staff were very friendly and helpful, reception has good staffing levels so check in/out is speedy and efficient. Overall the hotel is well appointed and is in a great location for the professional shopper and tourist but perhaps not the best spot for the City Slickers as the financial area is about 10 - 15 mins away by cab depending on traffic.As to the downside, I personally prefer a lounge/bar area close to the entrance foyer not on the 1st floor, not only for all we people watchers but to spot friends on arrival. However I reserve my main beef for the restaurant, not because it is buffet only, but because it is Halal. ( It does have a wine list howebver). So all of us who like a great English or American breakfast or just a Continental get used to Turkey or Beef Bacon not streaky/Canadian and no cold ham, prosciuttio etc either- for obvious reasons the owner, The Sultan of Brunei, is not a fan of these products. Regrettably you'll be hard pressed to find any mention of this on their website and there's me thinking that Singapore is a great example of transparency for SE Asia. In fact under Dining, the hotel maintains that it caters to every taste - some less than others maybe!! Apart from these it's got my vote.

<Author>Malingshu
<Content>Good but expensive I stayed at the RoyalPlaza for a week on business . The room was a little on the small side - okay for one person but would have got a bit crowded with two. For example, the tea and coffee making facilities are inside the wardrobe (!) and you need to have the door open to boil the kettle, but the door opens to the edge of the bed and there's no way to get past to the bathroom. The 'free minibar' is a bit of a joke - bottled water, a can each of coke and sprite, and 2 tiger beers. I was on the 8th floor and all the windows up to about the 9th floor look straight into a multi-storey carpark less than 10 metres away. The hotel is centrally located but this also means that the street outside it is extremely busy day and night. If you want to stay in Orchard Road keep in mind that there aren't many cheap eateries in this part of town.

<Author>mullet_rock
<Content>Excellent hotel! My friend and I just came back from a 4-night, 5-day trip to Singapore. We decided to stay at the Royal Plaza on Scotts because we have heard many good reviews about it and we got a pretty nice deal with asiabesthotel.com.We were not disappointed.Check-in was a breeze and the staff were very friendly. I recommend Karen at the front desk, she is very warm and willing to help out...very knowledgeable, too. Anyway, we were given a room on the 6th floor. We were also informed during check-in that the hotel was smoke-free and the rooms may not have a view. That was fine with us. We all knew this before we came to the hotel, so it was not an issue.The room itself was very clean, I think it was newly renovated. The beds were just right, as were the pillows. I love their slippers, though, very soft and perfect after a day walking through Singapore. Everything else was pretty standard. The bathroom was clean, but no bathtub. Personally, I like it better. I never use the bathtub in hotels anyway and the rain shower head more than made up for the lack of a tub, in my opinion. There had been a bit of a problem with the water heater once, though, but it was immediately fixed, so no biggie.A great touch was the free minibar and the free wireless internet if you have a laptop. If not, there is a complimentary 15 minutes daily use of internet at the business center (2nd floor) for guests. I don't think they're that strict about it, especially when there aren't much people who are waiting to use the computers.The breakfast at the Carousel was good, in terms of variety (and maybe quantity) and about average in terms of the taste and food quality. The ambiance was pretty cool, and the staff as always were friendly and very attentive to your needs (I dropped a fork and was immediately replaced even before I asked for it). As the other reviewers may have mentioned, the buffet does not serve pork. Sausages and bacons are made of chicken, beef or turkey. The hotel is in excellent location. Scotts Road is very, very near Orchard and about 3-5 minutes walk to the Orchard MRT. Beside the hotel is DFS Galeria and McDonalds and other malls just a few steps away. Overall, I would rate this hotel as above average. It falls a bit short on the food (taste and quality). BUT, as we paid SGD210/night including breakfast, we consider this as excellent value for money. So this ups my rating, definitely.  
<Date>Oct 9, 2007

<Author>Portuguesemanowar
<Content>Nice Hotel, one or two minor gripes The Royal Plaza has a great location being on the junction of Scotts Road and Orchard Road. If shopping is your thing then this could be the hotel for you. By prior arrangement the hotel agreed to let us leave some baggage with them whilst we went to Malaysia for 4 days. The concierge were very helpful and the check in was smooth. As there were 3 of us we needed an extra bed for our son. This took up a significant amount of the free space in the room. The room, a deluxe, is ideal for a couple but not a family of three. The bathroom was lovely, small and functional. Be aware that many rooms only have a shower and not a bath. On the negative side we found the free mini-bar a bit of a con. You get 4 soft drinks and 2 Tiger beers, just adding a couple of half bottles of wine would have made a difference. My advice would be don鈥檛 bother with the free mini bar and buy what you want at the 7-11 across the road, this will probably significantly reduce the room charge. The pool area was also a bit of a let down, there is a massive bar there but it is never manned, all they need to do is put a small fridge in the shaded area and fill it with bottled water. This would make ordering drinks less troublesome and allow you to quench your thirst without a half hour delay. The gym was advertised as state-of-the-art, it wasn鈥檛. They had done the old trick with mirrors to male it look twice the size, but the equipment on offer was limited and not of particularly good quality. The entrance foyer is spectacular, ornately decorated and at night with all the candles lit looks lovely. The bar areas are also very nice and the staff are very attentive, though again they have so many different promotions on drinks that it is very easy to get confused, this includes the staff. Breakfast was included in the price and was very good with an excellent choice of western and eastern menus on offer. All in all the Royal Plaza is a good hotel to stay in, the deluxe rooms are not suitable for families and the pool and gym could do with upgrading but our experience there was generally a pleasant one.

<Author>Berylina
<Content>Location Location Location Royal Plaza on Scotts in centrally located to everything you need in Singapore. Orchard Road is about a 2 minute walk, and most shopping centres are within walking distance. When we arrived the receptionist asked us if we wanted to upgrade our room for an extra S$30 per night, which included a bigger suite, free mini bar, and breakfast. We went for the upgrade and weren't disappointed. The suite was a good size, the breakfast was excellent, and the free mini bar was well utilized!The concierge were really helpful. They responded to our every request, no matter how obscure. Nothing was a problem for these guys. We saw an advertisement for a theatre production of The King  I, and asked concierge if they could give us some information about it. No problem at all, they downloaded all the info from the internet, then gave me exact instructions on where the nearest booking agent was located. One day we even asked them where a pet shop was so we could buy a goldfish for our friends fish pond, and they gave us a number of pet shop locations.One word of warning for smokers though - the Royal Plaza is a 100% non-smoking hotel. If you light up inside the hotel they will give you a S$300 cleaning bill. This was not an issue for us as we are non-smokers, however this was not pointed out to us when we made the booking.I would highly recommend the Royal Plaza on Scotts, and would definitely stay there again.

<Author>malolava
<Content>Fantastic experience and great value Taking a long time to choose between the myriad of Singapore hotels, we werent at all convinced we had made the best choice. On arrival at Royal Scotts however, we were thrilled with what we found in terms of service, value, and style. Check in was personalised and very friendly, and there was no problem with our checking in 4 hours too early. The room was small but newly renovated and decorated beautifully, had a fantastic bathtub and free internet connection. But best of all were the extras - a free all day mini bar including soft drinks and beer; free breakfast, afternoon tea and happy hour! We nearly didnt need to leave the hotel for food, although that would have been a shame as Singapore has some delicious hawker markets and restaurants. The breakfast buffet was only average, but the afternoon tea and happy hour offered lovely apertifs and finger food. The pool was nicely renovated but small, and our only complaint was that the poolside was booked out for a function on 2 of the nights we were there so we couldnt make as much use of it as we would have liked. I would definately stay here again for special and luxurious experience.

<Author>DoktorCB
<Content>Good Hotel, nice location I stood 4 nights at the Royal Plaza on Scotts in end July 2007. I'm coming since quite some years to Singapore and I have found my favorite hotel here already (and I didn't change my mind after this stay) - but this time I thought its time to try somthing else. The Royal Plaza location is very good, more or less in the center of Orchard road - just a few steps out of the hotel and you are in the middle of this shopping street. Even though after years I have discovered that nothing is cheap here. At least there are probably few places in the world where you have such a high rate of premium brand stores. Walking on Orchard is simply a good entertainment, even if you buy nothing. So this I consider as a big plus. Food: of course the hotel has a restaurant but on Orchard you find many more. I prefer Hawker food - which are these nice little boothes where you can order many dishes and share with your friends - and the best of it: outside with no aircondition! That Hawker food is typically less expensive and quite original is the other plus. So staying in Scotts you can easily walk either to a newly built Hawker center on Orchard - just follow the road down to the center of Singapore and you find it shortly after the visitor center on the left or you simply follow Scotts road down to Newton Circle - there is one of the most famous Hawker places in SG - but typically very crowded with tourists. For more original good food you better sit in a taxi and ask the taxi driver for more locations. I also like the Old Market very much which is in the business district. An old market hall from the early 1900's. Now lets talk about the hotel: checkin and the service are excellent and much above the standard. Very friendly and competent. The hotel itself looks every time I go there like just been build. I guess constant renovation is the key. The rooms itself are very tiny. The bathroom was my highlight: I don't like having a shower in the bathtub - I want a real shower and this is what you get here. Even the bathroom is very small, it has a nice and big shower with a real glas door to it where you can simply enjoy the morning. The rest of the room by the way is unspectacular. Nicely equipped to a high standard, with plat panel screen attached to the wall. But the most important: a high speed internet access for free. The free minibar you can forget about: 2 little water, 2 beer, 4 soft drinks. I only had water and 2 is in a location like SG simply too less. So I still have to buy it outside and carry it in the hotel.The pool and the gym: I didn't use both, because I had too less time. But I checked the pool area and I have to admid that it is ok, but much bejond my favorite hotel in SG. The pool is small, the pooldeck is even smaller and you have no view over Singapore. For just a bit of swimming ok, but not for spending there a full day.The breakfast: this is really good and can compete with my favorite one. But one big disadvantage: no pork! I like to have bacon in the morning, but here they either serve beef or turkey bacon - both not my tast. Beside this the food is excellent! Lots of egg choises and they make that fresh for you. The best waffles and pancakes I ever had in a hotel (of course at home that's better ;-). Fruits, salats, bread, cerials etc - as much as you like. And not to forget the asian bar with stuff what we consider as dinner. I can eat that for breakfast as well and it was so good! Most obvious I put on some weight :-)Finally I was very pleased with this hotel and by sure I will come back here. But even with this wonderful experience I do not change my favorite hotel in Singapore because of the nicer pool. But for just being there over the week where I have to work most of the time anyhow, this will be my clear choise in the future.  
<Date>Jul 29, 2007

<Author>TanyaMumOfTwo
<Content>Location, value, comfort and service! Excellent hotel. We have just returned from a 10 day family trip to gorgeous Singapore. (Plese see review for first four days at Raffles The Plaza and a Trip Report is still to come). The last two nights of our trip were spent at Royal Plaza on Scotts (RPS), July 11 and July 12.The excellent customer service began before we even left Australia when, after directly booking their best price for two Premiere rooms (1 X King and 1 X Twin, connecting) on the website, we received both confirmation and welcome emails. Then, within a couple of hours, I happened to stumble upon a significantly cheaper rate on another website (all others I'd seen previously had been more expensive than RPS own website offer) and contacted the hotel asking for their policy on Best Rate Guarantee. Whilst the cheaper price did not fully qualify (as it was not instantly confirmed) the hotel came back to me the next business day and said they would match the rate - this actually saved me about AU$300 as we had booked two rooms for two nights so I was very pleased and had a great feeling about the hotel right from the start.I was already aware that RPS was an inner city type of hotel which is what we needed for our two days of shopping. No views, but an excellent location near Orchard MRT and across the road from Far East Plaza and the Grand Hyatt with Tangs and Lucky Plaza just around the corner.The hotel is easy to miss from the outside but it is right next to DFS Galleria which has a large shop front. The lobby is very special and one very quickly leaves the bustling feel of the city behind within a few steps.Michelle checked us in and she was very helpful. Initially though the rate she had us booked at was not the cheaper one confirmed days earlier by email so luckily I had a copy of the email with me which she took to confirm the lower rate. Also our connecting room was not going to be vacant until closer to 10pm (it was 5pm at this stage as we had just arrived via ferry from Bintan - another review on this part of trip will follow). She did her best to see if anything else was available but as the hotel was full this was not possible. So we happily checked into one of our rooms and then went off to explore - upon our return just after 9pm our other room was ready and the rate had been sorted out. Michelle was still on duty and handled the situation very well.The hotel has recently been fully refurbished and the rooms were very clean and comfortable. Quite small (enough room to walk around beds, plus built-in good-sized desk and one arm chair) but we were expecting this so were not disappointed. As we had booked Premiere Rooms we had rooms on the 12th floor and each bathroom had a bath. The rain shower was the best shower I have ever had in my life! It was sensational! Much better than the one at Raffles The Plaza! The beds were comfy and pillows great. The flat screen TV was fantastic. The complimentary mini bar - beer, soft drink and water - was the best thing when you're travelling with two teenagers! Loved it!I never did see the pool so can't comment - although I understand it is more of a lap style. The buffet breakfast in The Carousel was very good but not excellent. Service was a bit erratic and toaster did not work well, but the tea (when it eventually arrived) was hot! I suppose we were spoiled by the breakfast at Raffles The Plaza and for many people The Carousel would seem first class.Our second day at RPS was actually my husband's birthday and at 9pm that evening there was a knock on the door and a tray with a spray of singapore orchids and a truly divine cake from the chocolate shop downstairs was delivered as a gift from the Hotel. It was accompanied by a handwritten birthday card. How special was that!! We organised a late check out on one of the rooms from 12 noon - 4pm @ S$20 per hour as our flight did not leave until the evening. This was easily organised when we checked in.Our check out was efficient and friendly without a hitch. All in all a wonderful choice and I will return there on my next trip to Singapore.  
<Date>Jul 16, 2007

<Author>MDTraveller1
<Content>Great stay on Orchard Road This hotel fits a great niche--the premier rooms are wonderful with large marble bathrooms, a nice business desk and luxurious bedding, the buffet breakfast is great, the service is outstanding, the location is perfect for Orchard Road people watching and shopping, near the botanical garden, etc, and yet is only a quick $5 taxi ride to downtown. The on-line prices were a good value--$200 a night for a first rate hotel including breakfast and the high Singapore hotel taxes in a nice location. Direct international dialing was a bargain. It is best suited for those who don't want the ambience of the massive five-star atrium hotels like the Pan-Pacific, which are set aside in sterile plazas. My only complaint is that they need an additional concierge with better restaurant and shopping advice. One strong suggestion is to avoid the dark, hemmed in lower floors--I moved from a depressing 3rd floor room to the 12 th floor and was happy.

<Author>mollygolightly7
<Content>Pleasant overall We've just returned from a five day stay at the Royal Plaza on Scotts. The hotel is located on Scott just off Orchard so it's very close to many conveniences like shopping, food, The Coffee Bean and Tealeaf/Starbuck's location war, and the MRT. Check in was quick and the curb staff was very attentive.  Our first impression of our room was that it was tiny so we were disappointed at that. It contained a king bed, a desk with a chair, a sitting chair, a bathroom with a shower, and a walk in closet with mini bar. The mini bar consisted of coffee/tea service and beverages (sodas and bottled water) which was replenished daily. The staff was happy to accomodate us with just water since we don't drink sodas (we left a note with the sodas and they were changed out the next day). The room had a mounted wide screen tv opposite the bed and the usual nice hotel things like iron/board, hairdryer, bathrobes/slippers, daily newspaper, laundry service, daily maid/turndown service.  The room was comfortable despite it's size and it was very clean. The nice details were the bed (which had a down comforter, mattress pad, and pillows) and the shower (which was roomy with a handheld and a big rainfall showerhead). It was nice to have the walk in to stow away our luggage and the car seat and the front hall was large enough to keep our stroller handy. One of the disadvantages was that there wasn't a table other than the desk. We have a toddler so when we needed to eat in there was no place to really feed her. And the obvious with a small room was that there was no place for her to roam aside from the closet. Also, when you used the faucet in the bathroom, the drain was really loud and there was a mere 1/2  clearance from the toilet and the bathroom door when it was opened so there's some maneuvering to be done to open/close the door depending on where you are in the room. The hotel has a couple of restaurants but we chose to eat outside of the hotel for a couple of reasons. The prices were high and there were better options for us nearby (we are vegetarian). There is also a pool and gym that we never got around to seeing or using. Overall our stay was pleasant. The staff couldn't be more attentive and the location was excellent. Although our room wasn't the best choice for our family, I imagine it would be great for a single person on business. We got a fair deal online so it made the whole experience fine.  Some pointers:*the key card is needed to use the elevators.*the key card is needed to keep everything on in the room: There is a holder by the door that powers the lights and tv. *check out the shower knob before you turn it on. There is a midline for off and turning one way gives you the handheld and turning the opposite gives you the showerhead. You can't really feel when you've hit the midline and a few times, while trying to rinse off my child's feet, we walked out of the bathroom with our clothes soaking wet.*there is a charge for local calls (although not much)*internet is free *the building is non smoking  
<Date>Jun 15, 2007

<Author>expatchick
<Content>Great Value - Great Location My family ( 2 kids - 3  4 yrs old) and I spent a long weekend in Singapore staying at the Royal Plaza on Scotts and we were very pleased with the whole experience. Check-in was quick, rooms were lovely; it has just been renovated and felt very modern and clean. The pool is great - perhaps not entirely child-friendly but lovely none-the-less. Best of all was the price - it was about half the price of most hotels in the area and it is in such a good location - moments to all the shops and restaurants on Orchard Road. There is also a complimentary mini-bar - includes some standard drinks - which is a very nice touch!! Only thing I would have liked is to have had a clock in the room - but apart from that - totally perfect hotel for a weekend away if you dont want to spend a fortune!!
