<Author>JulesAnne
<Content>Renovated but issues HiThere have been some great reviews about the renovated Royal Plaza on Scotts. I asked my TA to book me there. She got a rate of AUD 640 for 3 nights with a late check out. BTW RPS charges by the hour for late check outs.I joined IPrefer beforehand as it is their loyalty plan and the website says members receive an upgrade if possible. I was planning on staying again in October.I arrived at 11.00pm and initially they told me that I had to pay for the late check. I showed them the booking details. Then I asked them for the upgrade for IPrefer. That was definitely not forthcoming but they gave me a S$20 voucher for lunch or dinner. You need to ask. However, the restaurant will be closed on Monday as it was their Grand Opening.When I arrived in the room, it was tiny!!. Nothing like the pictures in reviews.By this time it was midnight. I immediately got wireless connection which was great. I then curled up in bed to read my book. Turned the overhead ceiling bed light on and all the lights in room, including the spotlight opposite the bed over the mirror. There are no bedside lamps. There was no way to read without feeling like you were in an interrogation room. Called front desk. They told me to move to other side of the bed and turn that light on. It is impossible to turn that light on unless the master on the other side is on which turns every light in the room on again. If you had a partner sleeping with you, he/she could not turn the light on to go to the bathroom. He would have to wake you to get you to turn the master on.The hotel engineer came up and checked it. He said that was how all the rooms in the hotel were wired. Duty manager phoned and apologised. Agreed this was a OHS issue. Turned lights off - the noise from trucks below and service kept me awake.Complained the next morning and they moved me up a couple of floors to a regular room. Realised that the initial room abutted the service lift and was two/thirds size of reg. room. Therefore the wardrobe was at the back of the bathroom and pushed the bed right down to the window.Still have lighting problem. Hotel provided me with a bed lamp which was perfect, but the wiring for the rooms need to be reconfigured.When I checked in they offered me breakfast at S$20 per day (net net) if bought upfront, otherwise it would be S$37.00. I bought the 3 breakfasts which were OK. However, the restaurant is Halal and the last morning I brought my tube of vegemite (Vegetarian yeast extract) and a waiter told me I couldn't eat it as it was Halal. Next time I will eat outside.I had a lot of appointments on the Monday and went across the street for dinner at the Far East Plaza. After doing a bit of shopping I was buggered. Arrived back at the hotel at 7.00pm to be told I couldn't enter as it was the Grand Opening. (Hotel) Guests arrived from the airport, joggers were waiting, A family had a baby who needed to be fed and changed, I needed to call my daughter before she went to bed in Australia. We all had to wait for half an hour while the festivities went on. Finally, the jogger rebelled and they were forced to let us into the hotel so we could get to our rooms. I think it would have been nice to have in someway included the hotel guests in the opening.On the positive side, the minibar is nice, staff tried to resolve issues and the beds are nice. Just insist you are not give Rm 516 or equivalent. I don't think you should get the worst room in the house because you are checking at a late time. I was always able to get a taxi.I ate in the restaurant on the Tuesday night and the food/buffet was very good.

<Author>Brian66
<Content>Highly Recommended It's hard to find a perfect hotel (except maybe the Peninsula in Bangkok), but this one does it's best. We stayed for 11 days which is a fair test. Check in was around midnight and the service was excellent. The entire hotel is non-smoking, which for us was a bonus. The room was a little small but most adequate, with a flat panel TV on the wall, a good work station, bar fridge, coffee and tea kettle and a very comfortable king sized bed.Try to get the odd numbered rooms as they have much better exposure to pool and view. (such as it is in Singapore.) We noticed a small amount of water on the marble floor when we first entered the bathroom. Next morning we called and they sent someone up to repair the leak. This hotel had just finished a major remodel, so you can expect the odd problem. In the end they moved us to the room next door, which had the same bathroom without the leak. I rank a lot of hotels by the shower and the rain shower head in these bathrooms was one of the best I've ever used.The rate included an excellent breakfast buffet, which catered to all the different ethnic meal choices very well. In addition they restocked the bar in our room every day and supplied high speed internet access (that worked) both at no additional charge.One little tip...they are demolishing a building located between the Hyatt and Marriot, which are across the street from the Royal Plaza. Although the noise was considerable 12 hours a day, it was not apparent in our hotel, but must have been terrible in the those two hotels.

<Author>Melnq8
<Content>Still the best hotel service in Singapore I've been a frequent guest at Royal Plaza on Scotts for well over two years. When the hotel closed for renovation in the fall of 2006, I very much anticipated the 2007 re-opening. The hotel rooms had become tired and run down and a full renovation was long overdue.Two weeks ago, the Royal Plaza re-opened for business, but to date, only floors 12 (Premier), 13, 14  15 (Club) are available to guests. All other floors are still in the process of renovation and are scheduled to re-open in March 2007.Anxious to check out the new digs, I booked a club room for two nights. I was given a room on the 12th floor (Premier), and was told the room was the same as those on the club floors above. I also had access to the club floor facilities.When I checked in I expressed concern about possible construction noise and was told the work would stop at 8 pm. This was not to be - on both nights drilling and hammering continued well past 10 pm. I contacted the front desk and the noise ceased shortly thereafter.The room was nice, but felt small. The bathrooms are bigger than before and contain separate tub and shower stall with rain shower. Understandably, the extra space needed for the bathroom was taken from the rest of the room.There were HUGE bath sheets (almost too big) and plenty of nice amentities in the bathroom. The room was nicely decorated and the bed was comfortable with a crisp cotton duvet. It felt completely geared to business travelers - there was a corner unit work station with an attached mini bar, and a single wing back chair. Gone are the small round tables and chairs, the vanity and small TVS. Now there are large 32 flat screen TV's mounted on the wall with a few shelves beneath the TV for storage.There's a safe and coffee making area in the closet. What I liked most - improved air conditioning system, comfortable bed, big TV with decent choice of stations to choose from and best of all, the same incredibly gracious employees I've come to know over the past two years. The service at the Royal Plaza is the best I have ever enountered anywhere. The employees are genuinely helpful and friendly. And get this, the entire hotel is now completely smoke free! What I didn't care for - room felt small and seemed designed for one person, there was no clock, and the corner work station overwhelmed the room, there was a lip on the door threshold leading into the bathroom which was easy to trip over.Breakfast, high tea and cocktail hour on the club floor are similar to before the renovation. Food choices have changed a bit, but it all seems a bit fussy - fancy nibbles displayed on tiny odd shaped china, small pieces of pastry tipped into delicate stemware, etc.Will I go back ? Absolutely, but I'll most likely wait until the rest of the hotel is open and book a non club floor room. The location of the hotel and the consistently good service are enough to bring me back.

<Author>ATraveller11
<Content>Good value for money, but very average overall. I stayed here for 4 nights on a long week-end away. The hotel is in the centre of Singapore鈥檚 shopping district and within minutes鈥?walking distance of several other big name hotels like Marriott, Grand Hyatt and Hilton, but a fraction of the price. This, together with its decent reviews, was one of the main reasons why I booked the hotel.The room was on the old and small side. The carpet was quite stained and tired, and could do with a good shampoo. The TV was small and old, and could do with being replaced. The shower curtain also could have done with being replaced. I wasn鈥檛 really expecting that much more for the price, which was GBP 72 per night.I booked a non smoking room with a king bed through Expedia weeks in advance, and for some reason they could only provide us with a non smoking room with 2 twin beds. This was quite annoying.The pool area was a bit small, but quite good though. It looked a lot newer than the actual rooms, and had some very nice touches to it like the finishing around the pool, and the matching pool furniture. The gym equipment looked very high tech and modern as well. I was not a big fan of sitting by the pool though, because there were far too many screaming annoying little children.Location is very good, just minutes walk away from all the major shopping malls on Orchard Rd. There are some bars/clubs that are very close by, like Bar None at Marriott and Brix at the Grand Hyatt, but nightlife in Singapore is scattered around everywhere. Apart from Clarke Quay, it isn鈥檛 really concentrated anywhere. To be honest there is nothing to do in Singapore besides go shopping. I would highly recommend Crossroads Cafe at the Marriott. It is a 5 min walk, and I liked it so much that I went everyday. The food was so delicious, and its fun to watch passers by walk up and down Orchard Rd. The lamb chops with mashed potato were the best I鈥檝e tasted in my life.

<Content>Good value for money, good service and a great location! I found this hotel to be good value for money at the internet rate I booked. The staff was pleasant and friendly and were particularly helpful when I returned soaked from a tropical thunderstorm after checking out on my last day. <Author>Calbiry
<Content>Free mini-bar, internet and a great location! For the price I paid, I wasn't expecting much from this hotel. But I was pleasantly surprised at what I received. The location is fantastic - all the shopping delights of Orchard Rd is right outside your door - the lobby was pretty special, and the staff were helpful. I found the porters particularly accommodating. The rooms have been well maintained and are clean and modern, and the free in-room broadband internet access and free mini-bar are major advantages. Sure, the mini-bar only has a selection of drinks, but it's a lot better than you would receive elsewhere. When I stayed, the hotel also had World Cup coverage, which other, more expensive hotels did not subscribe to. There were a few leftover items in one of the hotel drawers, the hairdryer was standard motel fare, and the shower was difficult to operate, but it was otherwise a fantastic hotel that I would return to and recommend!

<Author>HazelK
<Content>Free Mini mini-bar!! My husband and I stayed for three nights in February at the Royal Plaza. On checking in, we were asked if we had changed our booking as there was nothing on the system. It seemed that even though I had booked for the previous night and warned them that we would not be checking in until 7am the next day the booking had been cancelled as a no-show. This thankfully was soon rectified and we were allocated our club level room with complimentary breakfast for that morning. The hotel has a very grand entrance and is absolutely brilliant for the main shopping district of Orchard Road, with shops, food courts and cinema all within 300 metres. The room over looked a car park unfortunately, but we were not in that long every day. The best thing was the free mini (very mini) bar which contained 2 beers, water and soft drinks which was refilled each morning. We also had access to the exec lounge which was good for the snacks and cocktails in the evenings, but the breakfast was average. Overall, the staff were very helpful (but then everyone we encountered in Singapore was) so I would recommend this hotel if you can find a good rate. We paid 210 Singapore dollars,plus, plus, for a night

<Author>No_Fixed_Address
<Content>Enjoying Our Stay Greatly! We are currently in the midst of a six-night stay at this hotel. We obtained a very favorable rate for a stay on the club floor, which includes rooms with Broadband Internet, breakfast, afternoon tea, and a cocktail hour in the club room on the 15th floor. When we checked in (after midnight) the room clerk did not have a record and quoted us a much higher rate. We handed her our e-mail confirmation and the next morning everything was resolved immediately without question.Based on our previous stays in Singapore, Beijing, Shanghai, and Hong Kong, I have no hesitation in rating this hotel as a 4+. The only negative is a slightly musty smell in the rooms and corridors, but otherwise our room is comfortable and the service is great.The buffet breakfast on the club floor is more than adequate, and both afternoon tea and the cocktail hour include tasty morsels. There are also a couple of computers linked to the Internet in the club room with free access for those who did not bring laptops.Access to Orchard Road and the MRT is excellent. In summary, we are very pleased with the hotel and would not hesitate to stay here again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great location, good value, easy place to stay Stayed at this hotel for 4 nights with my two kids (10  7) on a school break from Bangkok. Hotel upgraded me to a Club Deluxe room (no extra charge) maybe because I requested for 2 king size beds (?). Agree hotel rooms are nothing fancy, but I paid US $65.00/night with breakfast for 3, which I thought was good rate for what we got. The location is fabulous - close to buses, MRT, etc. Service was good, breakfast buffet all the standard choices (cheese, egg choices, cereal, asian standards, good breads, etc.), room cleaned promptly, and nice touch to have free mini bar and apples. We ordered room service and enjoyed that too.All in all a successful visit. Might look for something with more character next time, but would stay here again, especially if could get this price.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Don't bother I stayed at this hotel just recently with my mother for short 5 night break. I booked the on hotel on wotif but was very disappointed when we arrived. The room was very small and the bathroom was like something that you would see in a budget hotel. I have also stayed at Meritus Negara and Raffles the Plaza on different visits to Singapore and the room standard of these hotels is far better. We did upgrade to the Club Deluxe room thinking the room would be better but all rooms are the same. The only difference is that you get breakfast included and some afternoon tea and a drink in the evening. All very well but we were never there at those times and the breakfast was terrible. I couldn't bring myself to eat anything except the dry old fried rice and some toast. The mini bar was a joke and on two occassions hadn't been restocked.Also without spreading accussations my mother had $50 go missing from her bag on the first day. Normally your room would not be cleaned until you have left for the day but they would come and clean our room while we were at breakfast which mean't we kept interrupting them and it was on one of these occasions the money went missing.It's states on the booking voucher that we would be entitled to 6pm checkout. We also had to fight for this. They said it was subject to availability. I found it very difficult to believe they were full and argued with them until they gave in.On a more positive note. The staff were very friendly and cannot complain about them. The location is also excellent for Orchard Road. I will definitely try somewhere else next time.
